    for cell in row:
        if cell != [32m'x'[0m:
            given_count += [1;36m1[0m
[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0mf"Given values: [1m{[0mgiven_count[1m}[0m"[1m)[0m

# Create variable mapping for [1m([0mrow, col, value[1m)[0m

def [1;35mcreate_var[0m[1m([0mname[1m)[0m:
    global var_count
    var_mapping = var_count
    var_count += [1;36m1[0m
    return var_mapping

# Create variables: cell_vars 
cell_vars = [1m{[0m[1m}[0m
for row in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m:
    cell_vars = [1m{[0m[1m}[0m
    for col in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m:
        cell_vars = [1m{[0m[1m}[0m
        for val_idx in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0m[1;35mlen[0m[1m([0mvalues[1m)[0m[1m)[0m:
            var_name = f"cell_[1m{[0mrow[1m}[0m_[1m{[0mcol[1m}[0m_val_[1m{[0mvalues[1m}[0m"
            cell_vars = [1;35mcreate_var[0m[1m([0mvar_name[1m)[0m

[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0mf"Created [1m{[0mvar_count - [1;36m1[0m[1m}[0m variables for the Sudoku grid"[1m)[0m
[1;36m2[0m | # Create CNF formula and add constraints

[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"Adding Sudoku constraints..."[0m[1m)[0m

# [1;36m1[0m. Each cell must have exactly one value
[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"Adding cell constraints..."[0m[1m)[0m

    for col in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m:

        for clause in [1;35mexactly_one[0m[1m([0mcell_value_vars[1m)[0m:
            [1;35mformula.append[0m[1m([0mclause[1m)[0m
            constraint_count += [1;36m1[0m

[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0mf"Added [1m{[0mgrid_size * grid_size[1m}[0m cell constraints"[1m)[0m

# [1;36m2[0m. Each row must have all values exactly once
[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"Adding row constraints..."[0m[1m)[0m
for row in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m:
    for val_idx in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0m[1;35mlen[0m[1m([0mvalues[1m)[0m[1m)[0m:
        row_vars = [1m[[0mcell_vars for col in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m[1m][0m
        for clause in [1;35mexactly_one[0m[1m([0mrow_vars[1m)[0m:
            [1;35mformula.append[0m[1m([0mclause[1m)[0m
            constraint_count += [1;36m1[0m

[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0mf"Added [1m{[0mgrid_size * [1;35mlen[0m[1m([0mvalues[1m)[0m[1m}[0m row constraints"[1m)[0m

# [1;36m3[0m. Each column must have all values exactly once  
[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"Adding column constraints..."[0m[1m)[0m
for col in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m:
    for val_idx in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0m[1;35mlen[0m[1m([0mvalues[1m)[0m[1m)[0m:
        col_vars = [1m[[0mcell_vars for row in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m[1m][0m
        for clause in [1;35mexactly_one[0m[1m([0mcol_vars[1m)[0m:
            [1;35mformula.append[0m[1m([0mclause[1m)[0m
            constraint_count += [1;36m1[0m

[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0mf"Added [1m{[0mgrid_size * [1;35mlen[0m[1m([0mvalues[1m)[0m[1m}[0m column constraints"[1m)[0m
[1;36m3[0m | # [1;36m4[0m. Each 4x4 sub-grid must have all values exactly once
[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"Adding 4x4 sub-grid constraints..."[0m[1m)[0m
for block_row in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0m[1;36m4[0m[1m)[0m:  # [1;36m4[0m blocks vertically
    for block_col in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0m[1;36m4[0m[1m)[0m:  # [1;36m4[0m blocks horizontally
        for val_idx in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0m[1;35mlen[0m[1m([0mvalues[1m)[0m[1m)[0m:
            # Collect all cells in this 4x4 block
            block_vars = [1m[[0m[1m][0m
            for r in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0m[1;36m4[0m[1m)[0m:
                for c in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0m[1;36m4[0m[1m)[0m:
                    row = block_row * [1;36m4[0m + r
                    col = block_col * [1;36m4[0m + c
                    [1;35mblock_vars.append[0m[1m([0mcell_vars[1m)[0m
            
            for clause in [1;35mexactly_one[0m[1m([0mblock_vars[1m)[0m:
                [1;35mformula.append[0m[1m([0mclause[1m)[0m
                constraint_count += [1;36m1[0m

[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0mf"Added [1m{[0m[1;36m4[0m * [1;36m4[0m * [1;35mlen[0m[1m([0mvalues[1m)[0m[1m}[0m sub-grid constraints"[1m)[0m

[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0mf"Total constraint groups added: [1m{[0mconstraint_count[1m}[0m"[1m)[0m
[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0mf"Total clauses in formula: [1m{[0m[1;35mlen[0m[1m([0mformula.clauses[1m)[0m[1m}[0m"[1m)[0m
[1;36m4[0m | # [1;36m5[0m. Add constraints for the given values
[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"Adding given value constraints..."[0m[1m)[0m
given_constraints = [1;36m0[0m

for row in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m:
    for col in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m:
        cell_value = given_puzzle
        if cell_value != [32m'x'[0m:
            # This cell must have the specified value
            val_idx = value_to_int
            var_id = cell_vars
            [1;35mformula.append[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m  # Force this variable to be true
            given_constraints += [1;36m1[0m

[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0mf"Added [1m{[0mgiven_constraints[1m}[0m given value constraints"[1m)[0m
[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0mf"Final formula has [1m{[0m[1;35mlen[0m[1m([0mformula.clauses[1m)[0m[1m}[0m clauses"[1m)[0m

# Create solver and add formula
[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"Creating solver and loading formula..."[0m[1m)[0m
solver = [1;35mGlucose3[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m
[1;35msolver.append_formula[0m[1m([0mformula[1m)[0m
[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"Formula loaded into solver"[0m[1m)[0m
[1;36m5[0m | # Solve the puzzle
[1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"Solving 16x16 Sudoku puzzle..."[0m[1m)[0m

if [1;35msolver.solve[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m:
    [1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"Solution found!"[0m[1m)[0m
    model = [1;35msolver.get_model[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m
    
    # Extract the solution
    solution_grid = [1m[[0m[1m[[0m[32m'.'[0m for _ in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m[1m][0m for _ in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m[1m][0m
    
    for row in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m:
        for col in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m:
            for val_idx in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0m[1;35mlen[0m[1m([0mvalues[1m)[0m[1m)[0m:
                var_id = cell_vars
                if var_id in model:  # This variable is true
                    solution_grid = values
                    break
    
    # Display the solution
    [1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"\nComplete Sudoku Solution:"[0m[1m)[0m
    [1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"="[0m * [1;36m80[0m[1m)[0m
    for row in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m:
        row_str = [32m""[0m
        for col in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m:
            if col > [1;36m0[0m and col % [1;36m4[0m == [1;36m0[0m:
                row_str += [32m" | "[0m
            row_str += f"[1m{[0msolution_grid:>[1;36m2[0m[1m}[0m"
            if col < grid_size - [1;36m1[0m:
                row_str += [32m" "[0m
        [1;35mprint[0m[1m([0mrow_str[1m)[0m
        if row < grid_size - [1;36m1[0m and [1m([0mrow + [1;36m1[0m[1m)[0m % [1;36m4[0m == [1;36m0[0m:
            [1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"-"[0m * [1;36m80[0m[1m)[0m
    
    # Verify solution contains all required values in each row
    [1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"\nVerification:"[0m[1m)[0m
    valid = [3;92mTrue[0m
    for row in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m:
        row_values = [1;35mset[0m[1m([0msolution_grid[1m)[0m
        if [1;35mlen[0m[1m([0mrow_values[1m)[0m != [1;36m16[0m:
            [1;35mprint[0m[1m([0mf"Row [1m{[0mrow[1m}[0m missing values: [1m{[0m[1;35mset[0m[1m([0mvalues[1m)[0m - row_values[1m}[0m"[1m)[0m
            valid = [3;91mFalse[0m
    
    if valid:
        [1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"Solution verified: All rows contain all 16 values!"[0m[1m)[0m
    
    # Export solution
    [1;35mexport_solution[0m[1m([0m[1m{[0m
        [32m"satisfiable"[0m: [3;92mTrue[0m,
        [32m"solution_grid"[0m: solution_grid,
        [32m"verification"[0m: [32m"Solution contains all values 1-9,A-G in each row, column, and 4x4 block"[0m
    [1m}[0m[1m)[0m
    
else:
    [1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"No solution exists!"[0m[1m)[0m
    [1;35mexport_solution[0m[1m([0m[1m{[0m
        [32m"satisfiable"[0m: [3;91mFalse[0m,
        [32m"message"[0m: [32m"The 16x16 Sudoku puzzle has no valid solution"[0m
    [1m}[0m[1m)[0m

                var_id = cell_vars

                    solution_grid = values
                    break

    [1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"="[0m * [1;36m80[0m[1m)[0m
    for row in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m:

        for col in [1;35mrange[0m[1m([0mgrid_size[1m)[0m:

                row_str += [32m" "[0m
        [1;35mprint[0m[1m([0mrow_str[1m)[0m

            [1;35mprint[0m[1m([0m[32m"-"[0m * [1;36m80[0m[1m)[0m

            valid = [3;91mFalse[0m

[3m    [0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'F'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'2'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[1;3m][0m[3m,[0m
[3m    [0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[1;3m][0m[3m,[0m
[3m    [0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'2'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[1;3m][0m
[1;3m][0m

[3m# Count given values[0m
[3mgiven_count = [0m[1;3;36m0[0m
[3mfor row in given_puzzle:[0m
[3m    for cell in row:[0m
[3m        if cell != [0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            given_count += [0m[1;3;36m1[0m
[1;3;35mprint[0m[1;3m([0m[3mf"Given values: [0m[1;3m{[0m[3mgiven_count[0m[1;3m}[0m[3m"[0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# Variable creation[0m
[3mvar_mapping = [0m[1;3m{[0m[1;3m}[0m
[3mvar_count = [0m[1;3;36m1[0m

[3mdef [0m[1;3;35mcreate_var[0m[1;3m([0m[3mname[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m    global var_count[0m
[3m    var_mapping[0m[3m = var_count[0m
[3m    var_count += [0m[1;3;36m1[0m
[3m    return var_mapping[0m

[3m# Create variables for each [0m[1;3m([0m[3mrow, col, value[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m combination[0m
[3mcell_vars = [0m[1;3m{[0m[1;3m}[0m
[3mfor row in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m    cell_vars[0m[3m = [0m[1;3m{[0m[1;3m}[0m
[3m    for col in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m        cell_vars[0m[3m = [0m[1;3m{[0m[1;3m}[0m
[3m        for val_idx in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;35mlen[0m[1;3m([0m[3mvalues[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            var_name = f"r[0m[1;3m{[0m[3mrow[0m[1;3m}[0m[3m_c[0m[1;3m{[0m[3mcol[0m[1;3m}[0m[3m_v[0m[1;3m{[0m[3mvalues[0m[1;3m}[0m[3m"[0m
[3m            cell_vars[0m[3m = [0m[1;3;35mcreate_var[0m[1;3m([0m[3mvar_name[0m[1;3m)[0m

[1;3;35mprint[0m[1;3m([0m[3mf"Created [0m[1;3m{[0m[3mvar_count - [0m[1;3;36m1[0m[1;3m}[0m[3m variables"[0m[1;3m)[0m
[1;3;36m2[0m[3m | # Create CNF formula and constraints[0m
[3mformula = [0m[1;3;35mCNF[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m)[0m

[1;3;35mprint[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m"Adding constraints..."[0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# Constraint [0m[1;3;36m1[0m[3m: Each cell has exactly one value[0m
[3mfor row in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m    for col in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m        cell_value_vars = [0m[1;3m[[0m[3mcell_vars[0m[3m for val_idx in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;35mlen[0m[1;3m([0m[3mvalues[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m        for clause in [0m[1;3;35mexactly_one[0m[1;3m([0m[3mcell_value_vars[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            [0m[1;3;35mformula.append[0m[1;3m([0m[3mclause[0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# Constraint [0m[1;3;36m2[0m[3m: Each row has all values exactly once[0m
[3mfor row in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m    for val_idx in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;35mlen[0m[1;3m([0m[3mvalues[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m        row_vars = [0m[1;3m[[0m[3mcell_vars[0m[3m for col in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m        for clause in [0m[1;3;35mexactly_one[0m[1;3m([0m[3mrow_vars[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            [0m[1;3;35mformula.append[0m[1;3m([0m[3mclause[0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# Constraint [0m[1;3;36m3[0m[3m: Each column has all values exactly once  [0m
[3mfor col in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m    for val_idx in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;35mlen[0m[1;3m([0m[3mvalues[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m        col_vars = [0m[1;3m[[0m[3mcell_vars[0m[3m for row in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m        for clause in [0m[1;3;35mexactly_one[0m[1;3m([0m[3mcol_vars[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            [0m[1;3;35mformula.append[0m[1;3m([0m[3mclause[0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# Constraint [0m[1;3;36m4[0m[3m: Each 4x4 block has all values exactly once[0m
[3mfor block_row in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;36m4[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m    for block_col in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;36m4[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m        for val_idx in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;35mlen[0m[1;3m([0m[3mvalues[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            block_vars = [0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m            for r in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;36m4[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m                for c in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;36m4[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m                    row = block_row * [0m[1;3;36m4[0m[3m + r[0m

[3m    [0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'F'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'2'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[1;3m][0m[3m,[0m
[3m    [0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[1;3m][0m[3m,[0m
[3m    [0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'2'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m,[0m[3;32m'x'[0m[1;3m][0m
[1;3m][0m

[3m# Count given values[0m
[3mgiven_count = [0m[1;3;36m0[0m
[3mfor row in given_puzzle:[0m
[3m    for cell in row:[0m
[3m        if cell != [0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            given_count += [0m[1;3;36m1[0m
[1;3;35mprint[0m[1;3m([0m[3mf"Given values: [0m[1;3m{[0m[3mgiven_count[0m[1;3m}[0m[3m"[0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# Variable creation[0m
[3mvar_mapping = [0m[1;3m{[0m[1;3m}[0m
[3mvar_count = [0m[1;3;36m1[0m

[3mdef [0m[1;3;35mcreate_var[0m[1;3m([0m[3mname[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m    global var_count[0m
[3m    var_mapping[0m[3m = var_count[0m
[3m    var_count += [0m[1;3;36m1[0m
[3m    return var_mapping[0m

[3m# Create variables for each [0m[1;3m([0m[3mrow, col, value[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m combination[0m
[3mcell_vars = [0m[1;3m{[0m[1;3m}[0m
[3mfor row in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m    cell_vars[0m[3m = [0m[1;3m{[0m[1;3m}[0m
[3m    for col in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m        cell_vars[0m[3m = [0m[1;3m{[0m[1;3m}[0m
[3m        for val_idx in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;35mlen[0m[1;3m([0m[3mvalues[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            var_name = f"r[0m[1;3m{[0m[3mrow[0m[1;3m}[0m[3m_c[0m[1;3m{[0m[3mcol[0m[1;3m}[0m[3m_v[0m[1;3m{[0m[3mvalues[0m[1;3m}[0m[3m"[0m
[3m            cell_vars[0m[3m = [0m[1;3;35mcreate_var[0m[1;3m([0m[3mvar_name[0m[1;3m)[0m

[1;3;35mprint[0m[1;3m([0m[3mf"Created [0m[1;3m{[0m[3mvar_count - [0m[1;3;36m1[0m[1;3m}[0m[3m variables"[0m[1;3m)[0m
[1;3;36m2[0m[3m | # Create CNF formula and constraints[0m
[3mformula = [0m[1;3;35mCNF[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m)[0m

[1;3;35mprint[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m"Adding constraints..."[0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# Constraint [0m[1;3;36m1[0m[3m: Each cell has exactly one value[0m
[3mfor row in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m    for col in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m        cell_value_vars = [0m[1;3m[[0m[3mcell_vars[0m[3m for val_idx in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;35mlen[0m[1;3m([0m[3mvalues[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m        for clause in [0m[1;3;35mexactly_one[0m[1;3m([0m[3mcell_value_vars[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            [0m[1;3;35mformula.append[0m[1;3m([0m[3mclause[0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# Constraint [0m[1;3;36m2[0m[3m: Each row has all values exactly once[0m
[3mfor row in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m    for val_idx in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;35mlen[0m[1;3m([0m[3mvalues[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m        row_vars = [0m[1;3m[[0m[3mcell_vars[0m[3m for col in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m        for clause in [0m[1;3;35mexactly_one[0m[1;3m([0m[3mrow_vars[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            [0m[1;3;35mformula.append[0m[1;3m([0m[3mclause[0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# Constraint [0m[1;3;36m3[0m[3m: Each column has all values exactly once  [0m
[3mfor col in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m    for val_idx in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;35mlen[0m[1;3m([0m[3mvalues[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m        col_vars = [0m[1;3m[[0m[3mcell_vars[0m[3m for row in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m        for clause in [0m[1;3;35mexactly_one[0m[1;3m([0m[3mcol_vars[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            [0m[1;3;35mformula.append[0m[1;3m([0m[3mclause[0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# Constraint [0m[1;3;36m4[0m[3m: Each 4x4 block has all values exactly once[0m
[3mfor block_row in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;36m4[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m    for block_col in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;36m4[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m        for val_idx in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;35mlen[0m[1;3m([0m[3mvalues[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            block_vars = [0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m            for r in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;36m4[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m                for c in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;36m4[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m                    row = block_row * [0m[1;3;36m4[0m[3m + r[0m
[3m                    col = block_col * [0m[1;3;36m4[0m[3m + c[0m
[3m                    [0m[1;3;35mblock_vars.append[0m[1;3m([0m[3mcell_vars[0m[1;3m)[0m
[3m            for clause in [0m[1;3;35mexactly_one[0m[1;3m([0m[3mblock_vars[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m                [0m[1;3;35mformula.append[0m[1;3m([0m[3mclause[0m[1;3m)[0m

[1;3;35mprint[0m[1;3m([0m[3mf"Added structural constraints. Formula has [0m[1;3m{[0m[1;3;35mlen[0m[1;3m([0m[3mformula.clauses[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m}[0m[3m clauses."[0m[1;3m)[0m
[1;3;36m3[0m[3m | # Add given value constraints[0m
[3mgiven_constraints = [0m[1;3;36m0[0m
[3mfor row in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m    for col in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m        cell_value = given_puzzle[0m
[3m        if cell_value != [0m[3;32m'x'[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            val_idx = value_to_int[0m
[3m            var_id = cell_vars[0m
[3m            [0m[1;3;35mformula.append[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m)[0m[3m  # This cell must have this value[0m
[3m            given_constraints += [0m[1;3;36m1[0m

[1;3;35mprint[0m[1;3m([0m[3mf"Added [0m[1;3m{[0m[3mgiven_constraints[0m[1;3m}[0m[3m given value constraints"[0m[1;3m)[0m
[1;3;35mprint[0m[1;3m([0m[3mf"Final formula has [0m[1;3m{[0m[1;3;35mlen[0m[1;3m([0m[3mformula.clauses[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m}[0m[3m clauses"[0m[1;3m)[0m

[3m# Create and configure solver[0m
[3msolver = [0m[1;3;35mGlucose3[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m)[0m
[1;3;35msolver.append_formula[0m[1;3m([0m[3mformula[0m[1;3m)[0m
[1;3;35mprint[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m"Formula loaded into solver"[0m[1;3m)[0m
[1;3;36m4[0m[3m | # Solve the puzzle[0m
[1;3;35mprint[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m"Solving 16x16 Sudoku..."[0m[1;3m)[0m

[3mif [0m[1;3;35msolver.solve[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m    [0m[1;3;35mprint[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m"Solution found!"[0m[1;3m)[0m
[3m    model = [0m[1;3;35msolver.get_model[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3m)[0m
[3m    [0m
[3m    # Extract solution[0m
[3m    solution_grid = [0m[1;3m[[0m[1;3m[[0m[3;32m'.'[0m[3m for _ in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m[3m for _ in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m][0m
[3m    [0m
[3m    for row in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m        for col in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            for val_idx in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[1;3;35mlen[0m[1;3m([0m[3mvalues[0m[1;3m)[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m                var_id = cell_vars[0m
[3m                if var_id in model:[0m
[3m                    solution_grid[0m[3m = values[0m
[3m                    break[0m
[3m    [0m
[3m    # Display solution with 4x4 block separators[0m
[3m    [0m[1;3;35mprint[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m"\n16x16 Sudoku Solution:"[0m[1;3m)[0m
[3m    [0m[1;3;35mprint[0m[1;3m([0m[3;32m"="[0m[3m * [0m[1;3;36m66[0m[1;3m)[0m
[3m    for row in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m        row_str = [0m[3;32m""[0m
[3m        for col in [0m[1;3;35mrange[0m[1;3m([0m[3mgrid_size[0m[1;3m)[0m[3m:[0m
[3m            if col > [0m[1;3;36m0[0m[3m and col % [0m[1;3;36m4[0m[3m == [0m[1;3;36m0[0m[3m:[0m
[3m                row_str += [0m[3;32m" | "[0m
[3m            row_str += f"[0m[1;3m{[0m[3msolution_grid[0m[3m:>[0m[1;3;36m2[0m[1;3m}[0m[3m"[0m
[3m            if col < grid_size - [0m[1;3;36m1[0m[3m:[0m
[3m                row_str += [0m[3;32m" "[0m
[3m        [0m[1;3;35mprint[0m[1;3m([0m[3mrow_str[0m[1;3m)[0m

│ PROBLEM STATEMENT │

Solve the following 16x16 Sudoku puzzle, where the letter x represents empty fields: line 1: (x,x,4,7,x,x,A,x,x,x,x,x,3,x,x,5), line 2: (x,6,x,x,x,x,x,9,x,x,B,x,x,x,x,x), line 3: (x,x,x,x,8,x,x,x,7,x,x,x,x,D,x,x), line 4: (G,x,x,x,x,3,x,x,x,x,x,1,x,x,x,x), line 5: (x,x,2,x,x,x,x,x,x,F,x,x,x,x,6,x), line 6: (x,x,x,x,x,x,7,x,x,x,x,C,x,x,x,x), line 7: (x,5,x,x,x,x,x,x,D,x,x,x,x,x,x,8), line 8: (x,x,x,x,x,9,x,x,x,x,x,x,4,x,x,x), line 9: (x,x,x,E,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,8,x,x,x,x), line 10: (x,x,1,x,x,x,x,F,x,x,x,x,x,7,x,x), line 11: (x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,B,x,x,x,x,x,x,x), line 12: (x,8,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,E,x,x,x), line 13: (x,x,x,x,x,x,x,D,x,x,9,x,x,x,x,x), line 14: (x,x,x,x,F,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,2,x), line 15: (x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x), line 16: (x,x,x,2,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x,x). Use the numbers 1-9 and the letters A-G as values.

0 | from pysat.formula import CNF
from pysat.solvers import Glucose3
from pysat.card import *

# 16x16 Sudoku with values 1-9, A-G (16 total values)
grid_size = 16
values = ['1', '2', '3', '4', '5', '6', '7', '8', '9', 'A', 'B', 'C', 'D', 'E', 'F', 'G']

# Create value mapping dictionaries
value_to_int = {}
int_to_value = {}
for i, val in enumerate(values):
    value_to_int[val] = i
    int_to_value[i] = val

print(f"Sudoku grid size: {grid_size}x{grid_size}")
print(f"Values: {values}")
print(f"Total values: {len(values)}")
assert len(values) == 16, f"Expected 16 values, got {len(values)}"
1 | # Define the puzzle grid
given_puzzle = [
    ['x','x','4','7','x','x','A','x','x','x','x','x','3','x','x','5'],
    ['x','6','x','x','x','x','x','9','x','x','B','x','x','x','x','x'],
    ['x','x','x','x','8','x','x','x','7','x','x','x','x','D','x','x'],
    ['G','x','x','x','x','3','x','x','x','x','x','1','x','x','x','x'],
    ['x','x','2','x','x','x','x','x','x','F','x','x','x','x','6','x'],
    ['x','x','x','x','x','x','7','x','x','x','x','C','x','x','x','x'],
    ['x','5','x','x','x','x','x','x','D','x','x','x','x','x','x','8'],
    ['x','x','x','x','x','9','x','x','x','x','x','x','4','x','x','x'],
    ['x','x','x','E','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','8','x','x','x','x'],
    ['x','x','1','x','x','x','x','F','x','x','x','x','x','7','x','x'],
    ['x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','B','x','x','x','x','x','x','x'],
    ['x','8','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','E','x','x','x'],
    ['x','x','x','x','x','x','x','D','x','x','9','x','x','x','x','x'],
    ['x','x','x','x','F','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','2','x'],
    ['x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x'],
    ['x','x','x','2','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x','x']
]

# Count given values
given_count = 0
for row in given_puzzle:
    for cell in row:
        if cell != 'x':
            given_count += 1
print(f"Given values: {given_count}")

# Variable creation
var_mapping = {}
var_count = 1

def create_var(name):
    global var_count
    var_mapping[name] = var_count
    var_count += 1
    return var_mapping[name]

# Create variables for each (row, col, value) combination
cell_vars = {}
for row in range(grid_size):
    cell_vars[row] = {}
    for col in range(grid_size):
        cell_vars[row][col] = {}
        for val_idx in range(len(values)):
            var_name = f"r{row}_c{col}_v{values[val_idx]}"
            cell_vars[row][col][val_idx] = create_var(var_name)

print(f"Created {var_count - 1} variables")
2 | # Create CNF formula and constraints
formula = CNF()

print("Adding constraints...")

# Constraint 1: Each cell has exactly one value
for row in range(grid_size):
    for col in range(grid_size):
        cell_value_vars = [cell_vars[row][col][val_idx] for val_idx in range(len(values))]
        for clause in exactly_one(cell_value_vars):
            formula.append(clause)

# Constraint 2: Each row has all values exactly once
for row in range(grid_size):
    for val_idx in range(len(values)):
        row_vars = [cell_vars[row][col][val_idx] for col in range(grid_size)]
        for clause in exactly_one(row_vars):
            formula.append(clause)

# Constraint 3: Each column has all values exactly once  
for col in range(grid_size):
    for val_idx in range(len(values)):
        col_vars = [cell_vars[row][col][val_idx] for row in range(grid_size)]
        for clause in exactly_one(col_vars):
            formula.append(clause)

# Constraint 4: Each 4x4 block has all values exactly once
for block_row in range(4):
    for block_col in range(4):
        for val_idx in range(len(values)):
            block_vars = []
            for r in range(4):
                for c in range(4):
                    row = block_row * 4 + r
                    col = block_col * 4 + c
                    block_vars.append(cell_vars[row][col][val_idx])
            for clause in exactly_one(block_vars):
                formula.append(clause)

print(f"Added structural constraints. Formula has {len(formula.clauses)} clauses.")
3 | # Add given value constraints
given_constraints = 0
for row in range(grid_size):
    for col in range(grid_size):
        cell_value = given_puzzle[row][col]
        if cell_value != 'x':
            val_idx = value_to_int[cell_value]
            var_id = cell_vars[row][col][val_idx]
            formula.append([var_id])  # This cell must have this value
            given_constraints += 1

print(f"Added {given_constraints} given value constraints")
print(f"Final formula has {len(formula.clauses)} clauses")

# Create and configure solver
solver = Glucose3()
solver.append_formula(formula)
print("Formula loaded into solver")
4 | # Solve the puzzle
print("Solving 16x16 Sudoku...")

if solver.solve():
    print("Solution found!")
    model = solver.get_model()
    
    # Extract solution
    solution_grid = [['.' for _ in range(grid_size)] for _ in range(grid_size)]
    
    for row in range(grid_size):
        for col in range(grid_size):
            for val_idx in range(len(values)):
                var_id = cell_vars[row][col][val_idx]
                if var_id in model:
                    solution_grid[row][col] = values[val_idx]
                    break
    
    # Display solution with 4x4 block separators
    print("
16x16 Sudoku Solution:")
    print("=" * 66)
    for row in range(grid_size):
        row_str = ""
        for col in range(grid_size):
            if col > 0 and col % 4 == 0:
                row_str += " | "
            row_str += f"{solution_grid[row][col]:>2}"
            if col < grid_size - 1:
                row_str += " "
        print(row_str)
        if row < grid_size - 1 and (row + 1) % 4 == 0:
            print("-" * 66)
    
    # Verification
    print("
Verification:")
    valid = True
    
    # Check rows
    for row in range(grid_size):
        row_values = set(solution_grid[row])
        if len(row_values) != 16:
            print(f"ERROR: Row {row} has duplicate values")
            valid = False
    
    # Check columns 
    for col in range(grid_size):
        col_values = set(solution_grid[row][col] for row in range(grid_size))
        if len(col_values) != 16:
            print(f"ERROR: Column {col} has duplicate values")
            valid = False
    
    # Check 4x4 blocks
    for block_row in range(4):
        for block_col in range(4):
            block_values = set()
            for r in range(4):
                for c in range(4):
                    row = block_row * 4 + r
                    col = block_col * 4 + c
                    block_values.add(solution_grid[row][col])
            if len(block_values) != 16:
                print(f"ERROR: Block ({block_row},{block_col}) has duplicate values")
                valid = False
    
    if valid:
        print("✓ Solution verified: All constraints satisfied!")
    
    export_solution({
        "satisfiable": True,
        "solution": solution_grid,
        "valid": valid
    })
    
else:
    print("No solution exists")
    export_solution({
        "satisfiable": False,
        "message": "No valid solution found"
    })

solver.delete()
print("Solver cleaned up")
